	shared_focus = PYT_air_stuff
}

### Military Focuses ###

shared_focus = {
	id = PYT_initial_army_reforms
	icon = GFX_focus_generic_strike_at_democracy1
	cost = 5.80
	available = {
		custom_trigger_tooltip = {
			tooltip = PYT_party_popularity_30_tp
			PYT = {
				check_variable = { party_popularity@ruling_party > 0.29 }
			}
		}
	}
	ai_will_do = { factor = 80 }
	x = 5
	y = 0
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus PYT_initial_army_reforms"
		army_experience = 15
	}
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_ARMY_BONUS }
}

shared_focus = {
	id = PYT_militia_roots
	icon = GFX_goal_offensive_army
	x = -3
	y = 1
	relative_position_id = PYT_initial_army_reforms
	cost = 5.80
	prerequisite = { focus = PYT_initial_army_reforms }
	mutually_exclusive = { focus = PYT_professionalism }
	available = {
		custom_trigger_tooltip = {
			tooltip = PYT_party_popularity_30_tp
			PYT = {
				check_variable = { party_popularity@ruling_party > 0.29 }
			}
		}
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 80
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			OR = {
				has_tech = superior_firepower
				has_tech = mobile_warfare
				has_tech = trench_warfare
				is_researching_technology = superior_firepower
				is_researching_technology = mobile_warfare
				is_researching_technology = trench_warfare
			}
		}
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus PYT_militia_roots"
		add_doctrine_cost_reduction = {
			name = cat_mass_assault
			cost_reduction = 0.5
			uses = 2
			category = cat_mass_assault
		}
	}
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_RESEARCH }
}

shared_focus = {
	id = PYT_call_to_arms

	x = -1

	relative_position_id = PYT_militia_roots

			}
		}
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 80
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus PYT_call_to_arms"
		custom_effect_tooltip = PYT_militia_tp
		hidden_effect = {
			load_oob = "PYT_militia_1"
		}
	}
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_MANPOWER }
}

shared_focus = {
	id = PYT_actual_conscription
	icon = GFX_focus_chi_army_reform
	x = -2
	y = 2
	relative_position_id = PYT_militia_roots
	cost = 5.80
	prerequisite = { focus = PYT_call_to_arms }
	available = {
		custom_trigger_tooltip = {
			tooltip = PYT_party_popularity_30_tp
			PYT = {
				check_variable = { party_popularity@ruling_party > 0.29 }
			}
		}
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 80
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus PYT_actual_conscription"
		add_manpower = 15000
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = disarmed_nation }
			add_ideas = volunteer_only
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = volunteer_only }
			add_ideas = limited_conscription
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = limited_conscription }
			add_ideas = extensive_conscription
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = extensive_conscription }
			add_ideas = service_by_requirement
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = service_by_requirement }
			add_ideas = all_adults_serve
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = all_adults_serve }
			add_ideas = scraping_the_barrel
		}
	}
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_MANPOWER FOCUS_FILTER_ARMY_BONUS FOCUS_FILTER_INDUSTRY }
}

shared_focus = {
	id = PYT_stock_the_villages
	icon = GFX_goal_arms_dealing
	x = 1
	y = 3
	relative_position_id = PYT_militia_roots
	cost = 5.80
	prerequisite = { focus = PYT_born_of_the_land }
	available = {
		custom_trigger_tooltip = {
			tooltip = PYT_party_popularity_35_tp
			PYT = {
				check_variable = { party_popularity@ruling_party > 0.34 }
			}
		}
		any_owned_state = {
			is_controlled_by = ROOT
			free_building_slots = {
				building = arms_factory
				size > 0
				include_locked = yes
			}
		}
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 80
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus PYT_stock_the_villages"
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				free_building_slots = {
					building = arms_factory
					size > 0
					include_locked = yes
				}
				OR = {
					is_in_home_area = yes
					NOT = {
						owner = {
							any_owned_state = {
								free_building_slots = {
									building = arms_factory
									size > 0
									include_locked = yes
								}
								is_in_home_area = yes
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction = {
				type = arms_factory
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = infantry_equipment_0 amount = 700 producer = PYT }
	}
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_INDUSTRY }
}

					size > 0
					include_locked = yes
				}
				OR = {
					is_in_home_area = yes
					NOT = {
						owner = {
							any_owned_state = {
								free_building_slots = {
									building = arms_factory
									size > 0
									include_locked = yes
								}
								is_in_home_area = yes
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction = {
				type = arms_factory
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				free_building_slots = {
					building = arms_factory
					size > 0
					include_locked = yes
				}
				OR = {
					is_in_home_area = yes
					NOT = {
						owner = {
							any_owned_state = {
								free_building_slots = {
									building = arms_factory
									size > 0
									include_locked = yes
								}
								is_in_home_area = yes
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction = {
				type = arms_factory
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
	}
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_INDUSTRY }
}

			}

		else_if = {

				has_tech = early_fighter
		    }

				uses = 1
				category = light_fighter
			}
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = fighter_equipment_0
				amount = 50
			}
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_dlc = "By Blood Alone"
				}
				set_technology = {
					iw_small_airframe = 1
					aa_lmg = 1
					engines_1 = 1
				}
				generic_early_fighter = yes
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = small_plane_airframe_0

					amount = 50
				}

				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = fighter_equipment_0

			}
		}
	}

	}

		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = disarmed_nation }
			add_ideas = volunteer_only
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = volunteer_only }
			add_ideas = limited_conscription
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = limited_conscription }
			add_ideas = extensive_conscription
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = extensive_conscription }
			add_ideas = service_by_requirement
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = service_by_requirement }

		else = {
			add_ideas = scraping_the_barrel
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			load_oob = "PYT_militia_2"
		}
	}

										building = industrial_complex

									is_in_home_area = yes
								}

						}

				}

					}
					OR = {

				add_building_construction = {
					type = arms_factory
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {

			swap_ideas = {

		OR = { ROU = { is_subject_of = ROOT } ROU = { exists = no } }

		OR = { ANG = { is_subject_of = ROOT } ANG = { exists = no } }

		set_global_flag = GRI_empire_rising_flag
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_core_of = BRZ
						is_core_of = KAT 
						is_core_of = STW 
						is_core_of = FEA 
						is_core_of = YAL 
						is_core_of = ANG 
						is_core_of = ROU
					}
				}
				add_core_of = ROOT
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FEA = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				ROOT = { annex_country = { target = FEA transfer_troops = yes } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { BRZ = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				ROOT = { annex_country = { target = BRZ transfer_troops = yes } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { KAT = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				ROOT = { annex_country = { target = KAT transfer_troops = yes } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { ROU = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				ROOT = { annex_country = { target = ROU transfer_troops = yes } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { YAL = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				ROOT = { annex_country = { target = YAL transfer_troops = yes } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { ANG = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				ROOT = { annex_country = { target = ANG transfer_troops = yes } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { STW = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }

	icon = GFX_focus_generic_strike_at_democracy1
	x = -3
	y = 6
	relative_position_id = PYT_erebus_steps_in
	cost = 4.40
	prerequisite = { focus = PYT_righting_old_wrongs focus = PYT_prepare_for_battle }
	available = {
		has_government = neutrality
	}
	bypass = {
		OR = { KAT = { exists = no } KAT = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
		OR = { ANG = { exists = no } ANG = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
	}
	allow_branch = {
		OR = {
            has_country_flag = PYT_heartlands_united
			has_country_flag = PYT_empire_founded
		}
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 160
		modifier = {
			has_war = yes
			factor = 0
		}
	}
	will_lead_to_war_with = KAT
	will_lead_to_war_with = ANG
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus PYT_take_katerin_and_angriver_neutrality"
		if = {
			limit = { 
			    KAT = {
                    OR = {				
			            has_government = neutrality
                        has_government = democratic
                    }					
			    } 
			}
			KAT = { country_event = { id = marschen.41 days = 7 } }
		}
		else = {
			create_wargoal = { type = annex_everything target = KAT }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
			    ANG = {
                    OR = {				
			            has_government = neutrality
                        has_government = democratic
                    }					
			    } 
			}
			ANG = { country_event = { id = marschen.41 days = 7 } }
		}
		else = {
			create_wargoal = { type = annex_everything target = ANG }
		}
	}
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_ANNEXATION }
}

	relative_position_id = PYT_the_grand_congress
	cost = 4.40
	prerequisite = { focus = PYT_industrial_modernisation }
	mutually_exclusive = { focus = PYT_the_industrial_heartlands }
	available = {
		has_government = neutrality
	}
	
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 110
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus PYT_maintain_agrarianism"
		if = {
		    limit = { has_idea = PYT_industry_4 }
			swap_ideas = {
			    remove_idea = PYT_industry_4
				add_idea = PYT_rural_economy_4
			}
		}
		else = {
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = { is_core_of = PYT }
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_manpower = 10000
			}
		}
	}
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_MANPOWER FOCUS_FILTER_INDUSTRY }
}

	x = -3
	y = 3

	cost = 4.40
	prerequisite = { focus = PYT_industrial_modernisation }
	mutually_exclusive = { focus = PYT_maintain_agrarianism }
	available = {
		has_government = neutrality
	}
	
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 110
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus PYT_the_industrial_heartlands"
		if = {
		    limit = { has_idea = PYT_rural_economy_4 }
			swap_ideas = {
			    remove_idea = PYT_rural_economy_4
				add_idea = PYT_industry_4
			}
		}
		else = {
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				free_building_slots = {
					building = industrial_complex
					size > 0
					include_locked = yes
				}
				OR = {
					is_in_home_area = yes
					NOT = {
						owner = {
							any_owned_state = {
								free_building_slots = {
									building = industrial_complex
									size > 0
									include_locked = yes
								}
								is_in_home_area = yes
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			    }
		    }
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				free_building_slots = {
					building = industrial_complex
					size > 0
					include_locked = yes
				}
				OR = {
					is_in_home_area = yes
					NOT = {
						owner = {
							any_owned_state = {
								free_building_slots = {
									building = industrial_complex
									size > 0
									include_locked = yes
								}
								is_in_home_area = yes
							}

					}
				}

			add_building_construction = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			    }
		    }
		}
	}
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_INDUSTRY }

		OR = { BRZ = { is_subject_of = ROOT } BRZ = { exists = no } }
		OR = { KAT = { is_subject_of = ROOT } KAT = { exists = no } }
		OR = { ROU = { is_subject_of = ROOT } ROU = { exists = no } }
		OR = { YAL = { is_subject_of = ROOT } YAL = { exists = no } }
		OR = { ANG = { is_subject_of = ROOT } ANG = { exists = no } }
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 110
	}

		set_global_flag = GRI_empire_rising_flag
		country_event = { id = marschen.64 }
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_core_of = BRZ
						is_core_of = KAT 
						is_core_of = STW 
						is_core_of = FEA 
						is_core_of = YAL 
						is_core_of = ANG 
						is_core_of = ROU
					}
				}
				add_core_of = ROOT
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FEA = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				ROOT = { annex_country = { target = FEA transfer_troops = yes } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { BRZ = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				ROOT = { annex_country = { target = BRZ transfer_troops = yes } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { KAT = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				ROOT = { annex_country = { target = KAT transfer_troops = yes } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { ROU = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				ROOT = { annex_country = { target = ROU transfer_troops = yes } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { YAL = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				ROOT = { annex_country = { target = YAL transfer_troops = yes } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { ANG = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				ROOT = { annex_country = { target = ANG transfer_troops = yes } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { STW = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				ROOT = { annex_country = { target = STW transfer_troops = yes } }
			}
		}
	}

	id = PYT_prince_of_heratlands
	icon = GFX_goal_government_icon
	x = 0
	y = 2
	relative_position_id = PYT_harmony_must_be_fought_for
	cost = 4.40
	prerequisite = { focus = PYT_take_feathisia_democratic }
	prerequisite = { focus = PYT_take_bronzehill_strawberry_democratic }
	prerequisite = { focus = PYT_take_romau_and_yale_democratic }
	prerequisite = { focus = PYT_take_katerin_and_angriver_democratic }
	available = {
		has_government = democratic
	}
	allow_branch = {
        has_country_flag = PYT_heartlands_united
		has_completed_focus = PYT_the_equestrian_model
	}

	available = {
		OR = { STW = { is_subject_of = ROOT } STW = { exists = no } }
		OR = { FEA = { is_subject_of = ROOT } FEA = { exists = no } }
		OR = { BRZ = { is_subject_of = ROOT } BRZ = { exists = no } }
		OR = { KAT = { is_subject_of = ROOT } KAT = { exists = no } }
		OR = { ROU = { is_subject_of = ROOT } ROU = { exists = no } }
		OR = { YAL = { is_subject_of = ROOT } YAL = { exists = no } }
		OR = { ANG = { is_subject_of = ROOT } ANG = { exists = no } }
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 110
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus PYT_prince_of_heratlands"
		custom_effect_tooltip = PYT_heartland_cores_tp
		set_global_flag = GRI_empire_rising_flag
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_core_of = BRZ
						is_core_of = KAT 
						is_core_of = STW 
						is_core_of = FEA 
						is_core_of = YAL 
						is_core_of = ANG 
						is_core_of = ROU
					}
				}
				add_core_of = ROOT
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FEA = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				ROOT = { annex_country = { target = FEA transfer_troops = yes } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { BRZ = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				ROOT = { annex_country = { target = BRZ transfer_troops = yes } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { KAT = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				ROOT = { annex_country = { target = KAT transfer_troops = yes } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { ROU = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				ROOT = { annex_country = { target = ROU transfer_troops = yes } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { YAL = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				ROOT = { annex_country = { target = YAL transfer_troops = yes } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { ANG = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				ROOT = { annex_country = { target = ANG transfer_troops = yes } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { STW = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				ROOT = { annex_country = { target = STW transfer_troops = yes } }
			}
		}
	}
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_ANNEXATION }
}

	id = PYT_united_at_last_2
	icon = GFX_goal_government_icon
	x = 0
	y = 2
	relative_position_id = PYT_the_road_to_herzland
	cost = 4.40
	prerequisite = { focus = PYT_take_feathisia }
	prerequisite = { focus = PYT_take_bronzehill_strawberry }
	prerequisite = { focus = PYT_take_romau_and_yale }
	prerequisite = { focus = PYT_take_katerin_and_angriver }
	available = {
		has_government = fascism
	}
	allow_branch = {
	    has_country_flag = PYT_empire_founded
		has_country_flag = PYT_truthahn_takeover
	}

	available = {
		OR = { STW = { is_subject_of = ROOT } STW = { exists = no } }
		OR = { FEA = { is_subject_of = ROOT } FEA = { exists = no } }
		OR = { BRZ = { is_subject_of = ROOT } BRZ = { exists = no } }
		OR = { KAT = { is_subject_of = ROOT } KAT = { exists = no } }
		OR = { ROU = { is_subject_of = ROOT } ROU = { exists = no } }
		OR = { YAL = { is_subject_of = ROOT } YAL = { exists = no } }
		OR = { ANG = { is_subject_of = ROOT } ANG = { exists = no } }
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 110
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus PYT_united_at_last_2"
		custom_effect_tooltip = PYT_heartland_cores_tp
		set_global_flag = GRI_empire_rising_flag
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_core_of = BRZ
						is_core_of = KAT 
						is_core_of = STW 
						is_core_of = FEA 
						is_core_of = YAL 
						is_core_of = ANG 
						is_core_of = ROU
					}
				}
				add_core_of = ROOT
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FEA = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				ROOT = { annex_country = { target = FEA transfer_troops = yes } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { BRZ = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				ROOT = { annex_country = { target = BRZ transfer_troops = yes } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { KAT = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				ROOT = { annex_country = { target = KAT transfer_troops = yes } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { ROU = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				ROOT = { annex_country = { target = ROU transfer_troops = yes } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { YAL = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				ROOT = { annex_country = { target = YAL transfer_troops = yes } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { ANG = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				ROOT = { annex_country = { target = ANG transfer_troops = yes } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { STW = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				ROOT = { annex_country = { target = STW transfer_troops = yes } }
			}
		}
	}
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_ANNEXATION }
}

shared_focus = {
	id = PYT_forges_of_war_2
	icon = GFX_focus_indy_industrial_tanks
	x = -1
	y = 1
	relative_position_id = PYT_arcturius_strength
	cost = 4.40
	prerequisite = { focus = PYT_arcturius_strength }
	available = {
		has_government = fascism
		any_owned_state = {
			is_controlled_by = ROOT
			free_building_slots = {
				building = arms_factory
				size > 0
				include_locked = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 110
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus PYT_forges_of_war_2"

					building = arms_factory

				}

					is_in_home_area = yes

						owner = {
							any_owned_state = {
								free_building_slots = {
									building = arms_factory
									size > 0
									include_locked = yes
								}
								is_in_home_area = yes
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}

				type = arms_factory
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {

					building = arms_factory
					size > 0
					include_locked = yes
				}
				OR = {

					NOT = {

shared_focus = {
	id = PYT_northern_war_2
	icon = GFX_goal_purge_opposition
	x = -4
	y = 1
	relative_position_id = PYT_empower_local_deities
	cost = 5.80
	prerequisite = { focus = PYT_empower_local_deities }
	available = {
		is_subject = no
		has_government = fascism
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 110
		modifier = {
			has_war = yes
			factor = 0.1
		}
	}
	will_lead_to_war_with = FAT
	will_lead_to_war_with = FAW
	will_lead_to_war_with = SRS
	will_lead_to_war_with = MNC
	will_lead_to_war_with = HAU
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus PYT_northern_war_2"
		effect_tooltip = { create_wargoal = { type = annex_everything target = FAT } }
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country_with_original_tag = {
				original_tag_to_check = FAT
				ROOT = { create_wargoal = { type = annex_everything target = PREV } }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = FAW }
			create_wargoal = { type = annex_everything target = FAW }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = HAU }
			create_wargoal = { type = annex_everything target = HAU }
		}
		create_wargoal = { type = annex_everything target = SRS }
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country_with_original_tag = {
				original_tag_to_check = SRS
				ROOT = {
					create_wargoal = {
						type = annex_everything
						target = PREV
					}
				}
			}
		}
		create_wargoal = { type = annex_everything target = MNC }
	}
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_ANNEXATION }
}

	id = PYT_attack_GRF_2
	icon = GFX_goal_generic_major_war
	x = 0
	y = 7
	relative_position_id = PYT_empower_local_deities
	cost = 15.80
	prerequisite = { focus = PYT_core_south_3 }
	prerequisite = { focus = PYT_core_frontier_3 }
	available = {
		is_subject = no
		has_government = fascism
	}
	will_lead_to_war_with = GRF
	will_lead_to_war_with = GFF
	bypass = {
		OR = {
			has_war_with = GRF
			has_war_with = GFF
		}
	}
	available = {
		any_owned_state = {
			is_coastal = yes
		}
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 110
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.1
			has_war = yes
		}
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus PYT_attack_GRF_2"
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = GRF }
			GRF = { country_event = { id = imperial.61 days = 7 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { GFF = { exists = yes is_subject = no } }
			GFF = { country_event = { id = imperial.61 days = 7 } }
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = { is_core_of = GRF is_core_of = GFF }
			}
			add_claim_by = ROOT
		}
	}
}
